 BPA director Nandani Rawal says, "this idea is not new

 We took this idea from there but this is the first restaurant of this variety in India
 unhone kaha, 'hamaara makasad doharaa he
 In a society in which we are seeing that our feelings towards others are diminishing, we want people to experience what life is like without eyes
 isse logon main unke prati samaj bad sakati he jinaki ankhon main roshni nahin hoti

 auto or taxi union kii mukhya maangen thi:-1
 The mobile app based taxi service was stopped with immediate effect
 2
 Prohibited the issuance of new taxi permits
 3
 Replacement of 15 year old black yellow taxis should be started as auto
 4
 Permit transfer process of autos and taxis should be simplified
 5

 ) The real strength of Tipu Sultan, known as 'lion of Mysore', was his rocket technology
 unke rocket angrejon ke liye anusandhan kaa vishay ban gaye the
 Former President APJ Abdul Kalam once described Tipu as the world's first rocket inventor in an event organized at Tipu Sultan Shaheed Memorial in Bangalore
 itihaas ke professor keke upaadhyaay ke anusaar tipu kii sabase badi takat unki rocket praudyogiki thi
 Tipu's army dispersed the British and the Nizams with rockets
 tipu kii shahadat ke baad angrejon ne rangapattanam main do rocketon par kabja kar liya tha or ve inhen britain sthit vuulavich museum art gailaree main pradarshnee ke liye le gaye the
 Born on 20 November 1750 in Devanahalli (present day Kolar district of Karnataka), Tipu Sultan's father's name was Hyder Ali
 vah bahadur or ran chaaturya main daksh the
 Tipu never bowed to the East India Company and fought fiercely with the British
 mysore kii duusari ladaai main angrejon ko shikast dene main unhone apane pita haidar ali kii kaaphi madad kii
 Not only the British, but the Nizams also lost dust
 apni haar se baukhalaaye hyderabad ke nizaam ne tipu se gaddari kii or angrejon se mil gaya
 When the British could not defeat Tipu in the third battle of Mysore, they made a Mangalore treaty with Tipu but despite this the British betrayed him
 east india company ne hyderabad ke nizaam se milakar chauthi baar tipu par bheeshan hamalaa kar diya or aakhirkaar chaar may 1799 ko shrirangapattanam kii raksha karte hue mysore kaa yah sher shahid ho gaya
 Tipu took command of Mysore after his father's death in 1782
 unhone sadakon sinchai vyavastha or anya vikaas kaaryon kii jhadi lagaakar apane rajya ko samrudh kshetra main tabdeel kar diya tha or yah vyapaar kshetra main kaaphi aage tha
 He laid the foundation of a dam on the Kaveri River
 isi jagah par aaj krishnasagar baandh he

 How BJP reached the pinnacle of power Arunachal Pradesh was known as the north-east Frontier Agency (NEFA) before 1962 and used to be a part of Assam
 saal 1965 tak is rajya kaa prashasan videsh mantralay dekhtaa tha
 In 1972, Arunachal Pradesh became a Union Territory and then on 20 February 1987 it was recognized as the 24th state of India
 centreshasit pradesh rahete hue arunachal pradesh main pehla vidhansabha chunaav saal 1978 main hua jisamen janata party ko jeet mili or prem khandu thungan rajya ke pehle mukhyamantri bane
 After this, in the elections held in 1980, 1984, 1990, 1995, 1999, 2004, 2009 and 2014, the Congress retained unanimous rule over the northeastern state and did not let its dominance diminish
 rajya main apana vajood banaae rakhane ke liye bijepi ko is dauraan kadaa sangharsh karnaa padaa

 The relationship of husband and wife is considered to be the biggest and sacred relationship and it is only to strengthen this relationship that the festival of Karva Chauth is celebrated
 karvaa chouth main mahilaayein pati kii lambii aayu or unki mangalakamna ke liye is vrath ko rakhti hai
 The earthen tots, from which they provide water, are called kokaravak

 Therefore, the importance of sieve on Karva Chauth is equally important

 This is the importance of the earthen caraway- Actually, water is first mixed with clay to make the caraway, which symbolizes water and land elements
 karave ko banane ke baad ise dhoop or hawa main rakhkar sukhaya jaataa he, jo akaash or vaayu tatv ke pratik hai
 After this the Karva is heated in a fire, thus the Karva consists of five elements
 isliye karave ko paanch tatv kaa pratik mana jaataa he
 Being made with the help of these five elements, clay carve has more importance than a stainless steel carve
 yahi kaaran he ki karvaa chouth ke vrath kaa samaapan pati apni patni ko mitti ke karave se pani pilaakar karte hai, taaki apane vaivaahik jivan main paanch tatwon ko sakshi banaakar khushhaljeevanaki kaamana kar saken
